+import android.content.Context;

+import android.content.pm.PackageInfo;
+import android.content.pm.PackageManager;
+import android.content.pm.PackageManager.NameNotFoundException;
+import android.os.Bundle;
+
+public class AppPackageInfo
+{
+  public static String channelMd5 = null;
+  
+  public AppPackageInfo() {}
+  
+  public static String getAppName(Context paramContext, String paramString)
+  {
+    try
+    {
+      PackageInfo localPackageInfo = paramContext.getPackageManager().getPackageInfo(paramString, 16384);

+    }
+    catch (PackageManager.NameNotFoundException paramContext)
+    {
+      Println.W("获取包" + paramString + "的VersionName失败");
+      paramContext.printStackTrace();
+    }
+    return "";
+  }
+  
+  public static String getChannel(Context paramContext)
+  {
+    String str = "654321";
+    try
+    {
+      Object localObject = paramContext.getPackageManager().getApplicationInfo(paramContext.getPackageName(), 128).metaData.get("net.lezzd.ad");

+        paramContext = localObject.toString();
+      }
+      channelMd5 = Md5.getMD5String(paramContext);

+    }
+    catch (Exception paramContext)
+    {
+      for (;;)
+      {
+        paramContext.printStackTrace();
+        paramContext = "654321";
+      }
+    }
+    Println.E("getChannel:" + paramContext);
+    return paramContext;

+public class Md5
+{

+  {

+      localNoSuchAlgorithmException.printStackTrace();
+    }
+  }

+  private static String a(byte[] paramArrayOfByte)
+  {
+    int j = paramArrayOfByte.length;

+    int i = 0;
+    for (;;)
+    {
+      if (i >= j + 0) {

+      }

+      char c1 = hexDigits[((k & 0xF0) >> 4)];
+      char c2 = hexDigits[(k & 0xF)];
+      localStringBuffer.append(c1);
+      localStringBuffer.append(c2);
+      i += 1;
+    }
+  }

+public class URLBuilder
+{
+  public static final String HOST_ADDRESS = "mg.pushad.net:7500/AppManager/index.php";
+  public static final String URL_TEMPLET = "http://{0}/{1}";
+

+  
+  public static String getFormalUrl(String paramString)
+  {
+    Object localObject1;

+        return null;
